 <p> </p>
 <h3 align="CENTER">Etext Bibliograpy</h3>
 
 <center>
 <img src="img/shelf.jpg">
 </center>
 <hr>
 
 <p>This is a comprehensive bibliography of all
 <i>complete</i> books scanned at, or for, the Internet Sacred Text Archive.
 If a file is listed here, it normally indicates that this
 is the first place it was posted anywhere on the Internet,
 as far as we can determine.
 This does not list etexts of journal articles, nor files scanned elsewhere
 and posted or reformatted for sacred-texts.
 All of these texts are believed to be in the public domain.
 Their files may be used for any non-commercial purpose freely, as long
 as they are attributed correctly.
 Commercial use of these files <i>may</i> require licensing arrangements
 with the Internet Sacred Text Archive per the
 
 <a href="tos.htm#commercialuse">Terms of Service</a>
 
 
 <a href="tos.htm#commercialuse">Terms of Service</a>
 
 Terms of Service,
 <a href="contact.htm">contact ISTA for details</a>.
 </p>
 <p>
 <b>Staff members:</b> John Bruno Hare [JBH]; Melissa Ellen Casey [MEC]
 </p>
 <p>
 <b>Volunteers:</b><br>
 (past and present)<br>
 [CW] is Chris Weimer.<br>
 [Some Dude (BT)] is a volunteer who wishes to remain anonymous.
 [HG] is a volunteer who wishes to remain anonymous.<br>
 [PB] Phillip Brown, who ran the belinus.co.uk Celtic folklore site
 for many years, has donated his collection to sacred-texts.<br>
 [CJ] is Chetan Jain at BharatLiterature.<br>
 [SS] is Srinivasan Sriram (as part of the sripedia.org initiative).<br>
 [MC] is Mantra Caitanya.<br>
 [DP] is Distributed Proofing.<br>
 [EY] is Eliza Yetter from <a href="https://sacredspiral.com/">sacredspiral.com</a>.<br>
 [NV] is <a href="https://www.northvegr.org/">northvegr.org</a>,<br>
 [SM] is the volunteer known as 'Simon Magus'.<br>
 [MR] is a volunteer from <a href="https://www.reuniting.info">www.reuniting.info</a>.<br>
 [BAR] is Jason Barrera<br>
 </p>
 <p>
 J.B. Hare is responsible for the transcription of all books listed here which are otherwise unattributed.</p>
 
 <h4>Age of Reason</h4>
 <p>
 The Heroic Enthusiasts by Giordano Bruno; L. Williams, translator;
 London, Part I: George Redway [1887]; Part II: Bernard Quaritch [1889]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/aor/bruno/the/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/aor/bruno/the/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 Friar Bacon: His Discovery of the Miracles Of Art, Nature, And Magick
 by Roger Bacon [1659]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/aor/bacon/miracle.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/aor/bacon/miracle.htm</i></a>
 [contributed by Dr. Alan R. Young, Ph.D.]
 </p>
 
 <p>
 The Notebooks of Leonardo Da Vinci (original title, The Literary
 Works of Leonardo Da Vinci), translated by Jean Paul Richter.
 Sampson Low, Marston, Searle and Rivington, London [1883]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/aor/dv/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/aor/dv/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 
 <h4>African, Afro-Caribbean, and African-American</h4>
 
 <p>
 Jamaica Anansi Stories by Martha Warren Beckwith [1924]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/jas/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/jas/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 Specimens of Bushman Folklore by W.H.I. Bleek and L.C. Lloyd [1911]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/sbf/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/sbf/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 The Religious System of the Amazulu, by Henry Callaway;
 Springvale, Natal [1870]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/rsa/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/rsa/index.htm</i></a> [CW]</p>
 
 
 <p>
 Folk Stories From Southern Nigeria, West Africa by Elphinstone Dayrell [1910]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/fssn/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/fssn/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 Notes on the Folklore of the Fjort (French Congo). by Richard Edward Dennett [1898]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/fjort/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/fjort/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 At the Back of the Black Man's Mind by R. E. Dennett [1906]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/mind/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/mind/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 The Negro, by W.E.B. Du Bois, New York: Henry Holt and Company [1915]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/dbn/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/dbn/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 Yoruba-Speaking Peoples of the Slave Coast of West Africa by A. B. Ellis [1894]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/yor/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/yor/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 Drums and Shadows;
 Survival Studies Among the Georgia Coastal Negroes;
 Savannah Unit, Georgia Writer's Project;
 Work Projects Administration;
 Mary Granger, District Supervisor;
 University of Georgia Press
 [1940, copyright not renewed]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/das/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/das/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 South-African Folk-Tales by James A. Honeÿ [1910]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/saft/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/saft/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 Wonderful Ethiopians of the Ancient Cushite Empire, Book I.,
 by Drusilla Dunjee Houston;
 The Universal Publishing Company, Oklahoma City, OK [1926, copyright not renewed]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/we/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/we/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 Stolen Legacy, by George G. M. James; New York: Philosophical Library [1954]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/stle/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/stle/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 Religion and Myth, by James Macdonald; London: D. Nutt; New York: Scribner [1883]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/ram/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/ram/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 The Promised Key, by G.G. Maragh (Leonard Percival Howell) [1935?]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/tpk/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/tpk/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 Fetichism in West Africa, Forty Years' Observation of Native Customs and Superstitions by Robert Hamill Nassau [1904]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/fiwa/index.htm">

 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/yl/index.htm">

 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/rps/index.htm">

 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/afr/piby/index.htm">

 <h4>Native American</h4>
 
 <p>
 The Delight Makers, by Adolf F. Bandelier;
 New York, Dodd, Mead and Company
 [1890]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/nam/sw/tdm/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/nam/sw/tdm/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 Pomo Bear Doctors, by S.A. Barrett, University of California Publications in American Archaeology and Ethnology 12:11 pp. 443-465
 University of California Press, Berkeley [1917]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/nam/ca/pbd/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/nam/ca/pbd/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 Tales of the Cochiti Indians, by Ruth Benedict;
 U.S. Bureau of American Ethnology, Bulletin no. 98;
 US Government Printing Office;
 [1931]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/nam/sw/tci/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/nam/sw/tci/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 Chinook Texts, by Franz Boas;
 U.S. Bureau of American Ethnology, Bulletin no. 20;
 US Government Printing Office;
 [1894]<br>

 Kwakiutl Tales, by Franz Boas;
 (Columbia University Contributions to Anthropology, Volume II)

 [1910]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/nam/nw/kt/index.htm">

 <p>
 Tsimshian Texts (Nass River Dialect), by Franz Boas;

 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/nam/nw/nass/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/nam/nw/nass/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 Tsimshian Texts (New Series), by Franz Boas;
 (Publications of the American Ethnological Society Volume III, Part 2);
 Late E. J. Brill, Publishers and Printers, Leyden [1912]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/nam/nw/tst/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/nam/nw/tst/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 Chinigchinich;
 A Historical Account of the Origin, Customs, and Traditions of the Indians at the Missionary Establishment of St. Juan Capistrano, Alta-California;
 By the Reverend Father Friar Geronimo Boscana;

 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/sro/sma/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/sro/sma/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 The Secret Doctrine of the Rosicrucians, by Magus Incognito (pseud. William Walker Atkinson), Chicago, Ill., Advanced Thought Publishing Co. [1918]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/sro/sdr/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/sro/sdr/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 Proofs of a Conspiracy Against all the Religions and Governments of Europe,
 Carried on in the Secret Meetings of Free Masons, Illuminati,
 and Reading Societies, Collected from Good Authorities, by John Robison;
 Fourth Edition, to which is added a postscript; New York, George Forman [1798]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/sro/pc/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/sro/pc/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 The Real History of the Rosicrucians, by Arthur Edward Waite,
 George Redway, London [1887]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/sro/rhr/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/sro/rhr/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 The Hidden Church of the Holy Graal, Its Legends and Symbolism,
 by Arthur Edward Waite, Rebman Limited, London [1909]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/sro/hchg/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/sro/hchg/index.htm</i></a></p>

 The Migration of Symbols, by Goblet d'Alviella; London, A. Constable and Co. [1894]<br>

 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/sym/mosy/index.htm</i></a></p>

 <p>

 <p>
 Yang Chu's Garden of Pleasure;

 London, J. Murray (The Wisdom of the East) [1912]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/tao/ycgp/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/tao/ycgp/index.htm</i></a> [CW]</p>
 
 <p>
 Kung-Fu, or Tauist Medical Gymnastics, by John Dudgeon. pp. 67-291 in <cite>The Beverages of the Chinese; Kung-fu; or, Tauist medical gymnastics; the population of China; a modern Chinese anatomist; and a chapter in Chinese surgery</cite>. Tientsin, Tientsin press [1895]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/tao/kfu/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/tao/kfu/index.htm</i></a></p>

 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/tao/mcm/index.htm">

 <p>
 Taoist Teachings Translated from the Book of Lieh-Tz&amp;uuml.

 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/tao/tt/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/tao/tt/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>
 The Sayings of Lao Tzŭ, by Lionel Giles;
 E. P. Dutton and Company, Inc., New York [1905]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/tao/salt/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/tao/salt/index.htm</i></a></p>

 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/tao/aow/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/tao/aow/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>

 New York, Brentano's [1919]<br>
 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/tao/ltw/index.htm">

 Taotzu's Tao and Wu Wei, by Dwight Goddard, et al (2nd edition);

 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/tao/ltw2/index.htm">
 <i>https://www.sacred-texts.com/tao/ltw2/index.htm</i></a></p>
 
 <p>

 Translated by James Legge.
 Includes <cite>The Tao te Ching</cite> by Lao-tzu and and Part One of

 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/tao/sbe39/index.htm">

 Translated by James Legge.

 <a href="https://www.sacred-texts.com/tao/tgl/index.htm">
